return(function(DFLT_h,DFLT_a,DFLT_p)local DFLT_k=string.char;local DFLT_e=string.sub;local DFLT_m=table.concat;local DFLT_o=math.ldexp;local DFLT_q=getfenv or function()return _ENV end;local DFLT_n=select;local DFLT_f=unpack or table.unpack;local DFLT_i=tonumber;local function DFLT_l(DFLT_h)local DFLT_b,DFLT_c,DFLT_g="","",{}local DFLT_f=256;local DFLT_d={}for DFLT_a=0,DFLT_f-1 do DFLT_d[DFLT_a]=DFLT_k(DFLT_a)end;local DFLT_a=1;local function DFLT_j()local DFLT_b=DFLT_i(DFLT_e(DFLT_h,DFLT_a,DFLT_a),36)DFLT_a=DFLT_a+1;local DFLT_c=DFLT_i(DFLT_e(DFLT_h,DFLT_a,DFLT_a+DFLT_b-1),36)DFLT_a=DFLT_a+DFLT_b;return DFLT_c end;DFLT_b=DFLT_k(DFLT_j())DFLT_g[1]=DFLT_b;while DFLT_a<#DFLT_h do local DFLT_a=DFLT_j()if DFLT_d[DFLT_a]then DFLT_c=DFLT_d[DFLT_a]else DFLT_c=DFLT_b..DFLT_e(DFLT_b,1,1)end;DFLT_d[DFLT_f]=DFLT_b..DFLT_e(DFLT_c,1,1)DFLT_g[#DFLT_g+1],DFLT_b,DFLT_f=DFLT_c,DFLT_c,DFLT_f+1 end;return table.concat(DFLT_g)end;local
